Variables {

    AbsDissipationRate {
        label     = "absolute dissipation rate"
        symbol    = "Abs-DR"
        unit      = "W"
        factor    = 1
        arsinh    = 1e-24
        precision = 14
        interpol  = arsinh
        material  = Semiconductor
    }

    AbsDissipationRateDensity {
        label     = "absolute dissipation rate density"
        symbol    = "w_Abs-DR"
        unit      = "W*cm^-3"
        factor    = 1
        arsinh    = 1e-10
        precision = 14
        interpol  = arsinh
        material  = Semiconductor
    }

    AbseNIECDJump {
        label     = "eNIECDJump"
